JOHANNES'S VISION
Johannes shakes his head firmly at the talk of guards and restrictions.
"Again, I must disagree. It needs no protection; its very nature resists any 
thought or attempt to abuse or misuse it. But instead, let it be freely 
approached, admired, touched even."
He looks at the Starjewel glowing on the altar, then at the assembled clergy 
and commanders.
"For those who will be summoned here by its call will be those who, like Soth, 
need the balm of godly judgment, of the freedom that comes from acceptance 
of truth. And we cannot stand in their way. They will come, and they will leave 
transformed. We have nothing to offer to aid or hamper their work."
 
SILENCE IN THE CHAPEL
Goldmoon, Elistan, Laurana, and the others exchange glances. Brother Marius 
opens his mouth to object, then closes it.
GOLDMOON SPEAKS FIRST
She approaches the altar, places her hand on the Starjewel, and closes her 
eyes. After a long moment, she withdraws her hand and turns to the group.
"He's right. I can feel it - the Starjewel doesn't need guards. It 
doesn't want guards. It calls to the broken, the guilty, the fallen. Those who 
need redemption will be drawn here, and we have no right to gatekeep divine 
mercy."
She looks at Commander Laurana. "This changes the tactical reality. The 
Chapel isn't a secured treasure vault. It's... a sanctuary. Open to anyone who 
needs it."
 
ELISTAN'S THEOLOGICAL PERSPECTIVE
The High Priest of Paladine nods slowly, understanding dawning.
"Of course. How did I not see it immediately?" He looks at Johannes with 
something like wonder. "The Starjewel is no longer just a relic of knighthood. 
It has become something greater through Soth's redemption - it's 
a sacrament of divine judgment and mercy."
"Think of what happened here: Soth sought judgment. The gods rendered it. 
He was released. The Starjewel purified. This entire sequence created 
something new - a place where the fallen can come to face truth and find 
peace."
He gestures to the Chapel around them.
"Guards would profane that. Restrictions would contradict the very nature of 
what this place has become. You don't guard mercy. You don't restrict truth. 
You simply... allow it to exist, and trust that those who need it will find it."
 
COMMANDER LAURANA'S CONCERN
"I understand the spiritual reasoning, but tactically..." She pauses, working 
through the implications. "If the Chapel is open, unrestricted, anyone can 
enter. Including Dragon Army soldiers. Including spies. Including those who 
might try to steal the Starjewel despite its divine nature."
JOHANNES'S RESPONSE? (Or does someone else address her concern?)
 
BROTHER MARIUS INTERJECTS
"Commander, with respect - anyone who enters with intention to steal, to 
abuse, to misuse... the Starjewel itself will judge them. Not violently, but 
spiritually. They'll be confronted with their own truth, their own guilt, their 
own need for redemption. They'll either be transformed or flee."
"The relic doesn't need guards because it is the guard. It protects itself through 
divine judgment. Just as it judged Soth, it will judge all who approach it."
 
GOLDMOON ADDS
"And consider this: if Dragon Army soldiers come here seeking to steal it and 
instead find themselves facing divine judgment of their own sins... we might 
convert more enemies through the Starjewel's presence than we could defeat 
in battle."
"A dark cleric of Takhisis who enters this Chapel thinking to claim a prize 
might leave questioning everything they've done. A dragonborn warrior 
seeking glory might find themselves weeping at the altar, seeking redemption 
for atrocities committed."
"Johannes is right - this place will transform those who come. We cannot 
predict how, but we cannot interfere with it either."
 
ELISTAN PROPOSES A COMPROMISE
"Perhaps this: The garrison protects the keep - the walls, the passes, the 
tactical position. But the Chapel remains open, unguarded, unrestricted. 
Anyone - resistance, Dragon Army, civilian, whoever - can enter freely and 
approach the Starjewel without interference."
"We document what this place is. We make it known throughout the region: 
Dargaard Keep's Chapel is sanctuary. Those seeking judgment, redemption, or 
truth may enter freely, regardless of allegiance. Sacred ground where violence 
is forbidden by divine authority, not mortal guards."
He looks at Laurana. "Your soldiers protect the military asset. The Starjewel 
protects the spiritual one. We trust Paladine and Mishakal to do their work."
 
LAURANA CONSIDERS
"So we hold the keep militarily, but the Chapel becomes... neutral ground? 
Open sanctuary?" She thinks tactically. "Actually... that might 
work better than restrictions."
"If word spreads that Dargaard Keep's Chapel is open sanctuary where divine 
judgment awaits, it becomes something the Dragon Army can't counter. They 
can't assault sanctuary without violating cosmic law. They can't prevent their 
soldiers from seeking it without revealing they're afraid of divine truth."
"And if their soldiers come seeking redemption and leave transformed... that's 
intelligence, potential defectors, and moral damage to their forces."
She nods decisively. "No guards on the Chapel. No restrictions. Open 
sanctuary. My soldiers protect the keep's perimeter and leave the Chapel to 
the gods."
 
THE DECISION IS MADE
Dargaard Keep Chapel becomes:
*	Open sanctuary (no guards, no restrictions)
*	Home of the Starjewel (freely accessible)
*	Place of divine judgment and mercy
*	Neutral ground where all may seek truth
*	Protected by divine authority, not mortal force
Word will spread: "At Dargaard Keep, where a death knight found 
redemption, the Chapel of the Order stands open. The Starjewel of Paladine 
rests there, calling to those who need judgment, who seek truth, who carry 
unbearable guilt. Enter freely. Face yourself honestly. Find peace or flee - but 
the choice is yours."
 
GOLDMOON LOOKS AT JOHANNES
"You see clearly. Not just tactics or strategy, but purpose. You understood 
what this place needs to become better than any of us who've spent lifetimes 
studying theology."
"That's... that's a rare gift."
 
CYRUS SPEAKS QUIETLY
"Johannes, you're right. This place doesn't need guards. It needs witnesses. 
People who will be here when the guilty arrive. Who will be present but not 
interfering. Who will see transformation happen and remember."
He looks at you seriously. "We might need to return here periodically. Not to 
guard, but to bear witness. To see who comes, who changes, who finds peace. 
To document what divine judgment looks like in practice."
 
THE SUN HAS SET
Darkness falls over Dargaard Keep, but it's natural darkness now - not cursed, 
not oppressive. Just night. And in the Chapel, the Starjewel glows softly, a 
beacon for those who need it.

into blessing.

NARRATIVE MOMENT - THE TRANSFORMATION
That evening in the Gallery of Ancestors, after witnessing divine judgment, the 
three of you feel the weight of what you've accomplished settling into your 
very beings.
Cyrus closes his eyes, and for a moment, you see golden light emanate from 
him - Mishakal's presence, closer and more tangible than ever before. When 
he opens them, there's a certainty there that wasn't present before.
"I can feel her. Not just as distant divinity, but as... partnership. She trusts me 
with greater power. Raise Dead. The ability to bring back those who've fallen. 
And Divine Intervention - the capacity to call on her directly when all else 
fails."
Kessa flexes her fingers, and you notice her movements are even more 
precise than before - that assassin's grace refined to supernatural levels.
"Everything feels... sharper. Clearer. I can see the threads of possibility in 
every situation now. And the songs-" She hums a single note, and the air 
shimmers with barely-contained magic. "The songs have deeper power. I can 
turn a battlefield with a melody. I can unmake enemy spells with a counter-
verse."
Johannes, you feel your patron's presence differently now. The binding is 
deeper, yes, but there's also... more. The fifth invocation slots into place like a 
key turning in a lock. Maddening Hex - the ability to spread your curse's 
torment to all nearby. And the fifth-level magic thrumming at the edge of your 
consciousness, waiting to be shaped.
The three of you stand in silence, looking at the portraits of Soth's family - at 
the testament to failure transformed into redemption.
You've become what this mission required: witnesses to divine will, 
instruments of mercy, and champions capable of changing the spiritual 
landscape of Krynn itself.

*	120 ft range, concentration, 10 minutes
*	Create impenetrable invisible barrier
*	Nothing can pass through (not even spells)
*	Incredible battlefield control and defense

*	Charm and control a humanoid

*	Great for interrogation, infiltration, or turning enemies

*	See and hear a target creature on same plane

RETURN TO HAVEN - ONE WEEK LATER
The party spent several days at Dargaard Keep helping establish the garrison, 
then returned to Haven. The debriefing with Commander Laurana was 
extensive - the full story of the curse-breaking, the divine judgment, and the 
establishment of the sanctuary.
Word has spread quickly through the resistance: Dargaard Keep is secured. 
The three-hundred-year curse is broken. A death knight found redemption.
The party has become legendary within Haven's ranks. Soldiers salute as you 
pass. Clerics seek your counsel. Even grizzled veterans look at you with 
newfound respect.
 
COMMANDER LAURANA'S OFFICE - MORNING
You're summoned to Laurana's command tent. When you arrive, she's 
studying a map of the region with several markers indicating Dragon Army 
positions.
She looks up as you enter.
"Welcome back. I trust you've had time to rest and process everything that 
happened at Dargaard Keep?"
She doesn't wait for an answer - you can tell something urgent is on her mind.
"We have a situation. Multiple situations, actually. The resistance is growing 
stronger, which means the Dragon Army is adapting. We're seeing increased 
activity on several fronts."
She gestures to the map.
"I have three mission options for you. All are critical, all are dangerous, and all 
require the kind of... unconventional thinking you've demonstrated."
She taps three locations on the map:
 
MISSION OPTION 1: PALANTHAS INTRIGUE
"Our Warehouse 47 in Palanthas has detected unusual activity. Grimbold, 
your caretaker, sent word via magical courier that Dragon Army agents have 
been asking questions about the warehouse's owners. Specifically about you 
three."
"Additionally, there are rumors that a high-ranking Dragon Army officer is 
secretly negotiating with Palanthas city officials - possibly trying to bring the 
neutral city into the Dragon Army's fold through diplomacy rather than force."
"If Palanthas falls to the Dragon Army without a fight, we lose our only major 
neutral staging ground, and the entire coastal region becomes theirs."
Mission objective:
*	Investigate Dragon Army interest in your identities
*	Uncover and potentially sabotage the diplomatic negotiations
*	Maintain Palanthas's neutrality
Complexity: Political intrigue, investigation, potential high-society 
infiltration Danger Level: Moderate combat, high consequences for 
failure Duration: 2-3 weeks estimated
 
MISSION OPTION 2: THE BLOOD SEA CROSSING
"We've received reports from refugees fleeing Dragon Army-occupied 
territories in the east. They speak of a safe passage being organized - ships 
crossing the Blood Sea of Ishan to bring civilians to safer lands."
"But the Dragon Army has noticed. They're positioning naval forces to 
intercept and destroy these refugee ships. Hundreds, possibly thousands of 
civilians will die unless someone can protect the crossing or eliminate the 
Dragon Army naval threat."
"This isn't a stealth mission. This is direct action against a Dragon Army naval 
squadron - likely 5-8 warships, well-armed, with dragonborn marines and 
possibly a dragon providing air support."
Mission objective:
*	Protect refugee ships during Blood Sea crossing
*	Eliminate or disable Dragon Army naval squadron
*	Ensure maximum civilian survival
Complexity: Naval combat, large-scale engagement, protecting civilians 
under fire Danger Level: High combat, high casualty risk Duration: 1-2 
weeks estimated
 
MISSION OPTION 3: THE NIGHTMARE VAULT
"This one's... different. We've had reports from scouts near the ruins of Xak 
Tsaroth - a city destroyed in the Cataclysm. The Dragon Army has been 
excavating something there. Something old."
"Our intelligence suggests they're searching for pre-Cataclysm magical 
artifacts. Specifically, weapons or relics that could tip the balance of power. 
We don't know exactly what they've found, but the excavation site is heavily 
guarded and there's been... strange activity. Scouts report nightmares, 
hallucinations, and one team went missing entirely."
"This feels like another Dargaard Keep situation - something supernatural that 
the Dragon Army is trying to exploit or control."
Mission objective:
*	Infiltrate Xak Tsaroth ruins
*	Determine what the Dragon Army is excavating
*	Secure or destroy whatever they've found
*	Survive whatever supernatural threat is causing the anomalies
Complexity: Dungeon delve, supernatural threats, unknown 
dangers Danger Level: Moderate to high combat, high unknown 
risk Duration: 2-3 weeks estimated

DAY 1-2: TRAVEL SOUTHEAST
The journey toward Xak Tsaroth takes you through increasingly desolate 
terrain. The land here still bears scars from the Cataclysm - twisted rock 
formations, dead forests, and an oppressive atmosphere.
On the evening of Day 2, you make camp in a sheltered ravine. The ruins of 
Xak Tsaroth are still three days away, but this seems like a good time to 
contact Khisanth.
JOHANNES - KHISANTH'S SCALE
You retrieve the black dragon scale - large as a dinner plate, gleaming with an 
oily iridescence even in firelight. Khisanth gave this to you after your alliance 
was forged, with instructions on how to contact her.
The scale is warm to the touch and pulses faintly with draconic magic.
To activate it, Johannes needs to:
*	Hold the scale
*	Speak Khisanth's name clearly
*	State the nature of the contact (question, warning, request for meeting, 
etc.)
The scale allows one-way communication - you can speak to her, but she 
responds via magical sending that only the scale-holder hears.
What does Johannes say to Khisanth?

*	Brief greeting acknowledging your alliance
*	Inform her Dragon Army is excavating deep ruins at Xak Tsaroth

Dec 10
CONTACTING KHISANTH
Johannes holds the black dragon scale, feeling its warmth and the pulse of 
draconic magic within. He speaks clearly:
"Khisanth. Johannes Constantinius. The Dragon Army is excavating the deep 
ruins beneath Xak Tsaroth's Temple District - sections that were flooded or 
collapsed when we last met. They're experiencing supernatural effects: 
nightmares, hallucinations, paranoia. We're en route to investigate and stop 
them. What do you know about what lies in those lower levels?"
The scale grows hot, almost uncomfortably so, then Khisanth's voice resonates 
directly into Johannes's mind - not gentle, but controlled, like distant thunder:
"JOHANNNES CONSTANTINIUS. YOUR TIMING IS... 
CONVENIENT."
"I occupied those ruins for three centuries. The upper levels, the 
accessible chambers, the flooded sections - all known to me. But 
the DEEPEST vaults beneath the Temple of Huerzyd remained 
sealed. Sealed by the Cataclysm itself. Sealed by divine judgment."
"I attempted to breach them twice in three hundred years. Both 
times, the nightmares drove even ME back. What lies below is OLD. 
Pre-Cataclysm. Pre-Kingpriest. Perhaps pre-EMPIRE."
A pause, and you can almost hear her considering whether to share more.
"The Dragon Army excavates what I could not reach. Either they 
are FOOLS, or they possess knowledge I lack. Neither possibility 
pleases me."
"What I know: The Temple of Huerzyd was dedicated to a god 
whose name was STRUCK from history. The priests there dealt in... 
containment. Binding. They imprisoned things that should not 
exist. When the Cataclysm struck, their wards held - barely. What 
lies below is CONTAINED, but three hundred years of isolation 
may have weakened those bindings."
"If the Dragon Army breaches the final seals, they will release 
something that PREDATES THE GODS OF KRYNN. Something the 
ancient priests deemed too dangerous to destroy, so they 
IMPRISONED instead."
"My counsel: STOP THEM. Seal the excavation. Bury it again. Do 
NOT attempt to claim whatever lies below for your resistance. 
Some weapons are not worth wielding."
"And Johannes? If you FAIL, if they breach the seals and release 
what lies dormant... RUN. Do not fight it. Do not study it. RUN, and 
warn your commanders that the Dragon Army has unleashed 
something beyond their control."
"Our alliance stands. I will not interfere with your mission. But I 
will also not AID. What you face in those depths is YOUR concern 
now. I am well satisfied with Pax Tharkas and have no desire to 
return to those cursed ruins."
"One final warning: The nightmares you experience will show you 
TRUTH. Terrible truth. The entity below feeds on knowledge of 
what WAS and what COULD HAVE BEEN. Steel your minds, or you 
will break before you even reach the seals."
The scale cools. The connection ends.
 
CYRUS AND KESSA'S REACTIONS
Both have been watching Johannes during the contact, seeing his expression 
shift as he receives Khisanth's message.
Cyrus: "That looked... ominous. What did she say?"
Kessa: "And why do you look like you just got told we're walking into 
something that scared off an ancient dragon?"
 
JOHANNES - WHAT DO YOU TELL YOUR COMPANIONS?
And more importantly: Does this intelligence change your approach to 
the mission?
You now know:
*	What's below predates even the gods of Krynn
*	It was imprisoned by ancient priests, not destroyed

*	Even Khisanth was driven back by the nightmares twice
*	The Dragon Army is close to breaching the final containment
*	Khisanth's advice: Seal it, bury it, don't try to claim it
Do you:
1.	Continue as planned - stop the Dragon Army, deal with whatever's

2.	Adjust strategy - focus on collapsing the excavation rather than

3.	Request reinforcements - send word back to Haven that this is

4.	Gather more intelligence - scout thoroughly before committing
What's your call?
Continue as planned...
Dec 10
JOHANNES RELAYS KHISANTH'S WARNING
Johannes shares Khisanth's message with Cyrus and Kessa - the ancient

KESSA'S RESPONSE:
"So we're walking into a place that's been sealed for over three hundred years,

She checks her weapons methodically. "Well, at least we know what we're

CYRUS'S ASSESSMENT:
"Entities that predate the gods... binding magic from civilizations lost to

perhaps divine power can re-seal it."
He grips his holy symbol. "We continue. We stop the Dragon Army. We assess 
the seals. And if necessary, we bury it all and let it stay buried for another 
thousand years."
 
DAY 3-5: APPROACH TO XAK TSAROTH
The final days of travel take you through increasingly twisted terrain. The 
closer you get to Xak Tsaroth, the more oppressive the atmosphere becomes.
Night 3: Cyrus has disturbing dreams - visions of Xak Tsaroth before the 
Cataclysm, a magnificent city full of life, then the moment of destruction. He 
wakes gasping.
Night 4: Kessa dreams of the excavation site - sees Dragon Army soldiers 
digging, their faces twisted with exhaustion and fear, and 
something moving in the darkness below them.
Night 5: Johannes dreams of the sealed chamber - ancient priests performing 
binding rituals, their faces desperate, chanting in languages that hurt to hear 
even in dreams. One priest looks directly at him and mouths: "It must never 
wake."
The nightmares are beginning. And you're still a day away from the ruins.

Nightmares. What about my ring of mind shielding?
Dec 10
EXCELLENT POINT - RING OF MIND SHIELDING
You're absolutely right! Johannes wears the Ring of Mind Shielding, which 
has these properties:
*	Your thoughts can't be read by telepathy or other means
*	You can't be compelled to tell the truth by magic
*	You can't be determined to be lying by magic
*	While wearing this ring, you are immune to magic that allows 
other creatures to read your thoughts, determine whether you 
are lying, know your alignment, or know your creature type
The nightmares are almost certainly magical/psychic in nature - an entity that 
"feeds on knowledge" trying to invade minds.
CORRECTING THE NIGHTMARE EFFECTS:
Johannes: The Ring of Mind Shielding protects you completely. You've had 
no nightmares. Your sleep has been peaceful and undisturbed. The entity 
below cannot touch your mind while you wear the ring.
Cyrus & Kessa: Both experienced the nightmares as described - visions of 
the past, the excavation, the sealed chamber.
 
THIS CHANGES THE TACTICAL PICTURE
Cyrus speaks as you observe the Dragon Army camp:
"Johannes, you haven't had the nightmares, have you? The ring - it's 
protecting you from whatever's down there trying to get into our heads."
He looks exhausted from days of disturbed sleep. "Kessa and I have been 
seeing things. Visions of the past, of what's being dug up. It's... draining. But 
you're clear-headed."
Kessa adds:
"Which means when we go down there, you're our anchor. If Cyrus and I start 
seeing things, hearing things, losing track of what's real - you'll be the one who 
can tell us we're wrong. The one it can't touch."
She manages a tired smile. "Lucky you get to be the stable one for once."
 
STRATEGIC ADVANTAGE:
Johannes being immune to the psychic/nightmare effects means:
*	You can scout the excavation site without mental interference
*	You can lead the team through areas where hallucinations are strongest
*	You're protected from whatever entity is causing the effects
*	You can tell when Cyrus/Kessa are being influenced
However: The ring only protects you. Your companions are still vulnerable.
 
BACK TO TACTICAL PLANNING

4.	Something else
What's the plan?
Observe

"It will remain there, at the site of its prison, until something disturbs it. And

DAY 11 - RETURN TO HAVEN

DETOUR TO AK-THYLN
The route to Palanthas takes you through the Ak-Thyln region anyway - only

DAY 3 OF TRAVEL - ARRIVAL AT AK-THYLN
The coastal town looks prosperous and peaceful - a stark contrast to when you 
first arrived here before the Flotsam operation. The Dragon Army invasion 
that would have devastated this region never came, thanks to your destruction 
of the fleet.
Citizens recognize you as you pass through - grateful nods, a few waves, 
children pointing excitedly. You're heroes here.
 
MASTER KELDIN'S WORKSHOP - AFTERNOON
The workshop is exactly as you remember - multiple chimneys smoking, the 
hum of arcane machinery, protective wards shimmering on windows and 
doors.
When you knock, Keldin's voice booms from inside: "It's open! Unless you're 
Dragon Army, in which case it's very much closed and possibly explosive!"
You enter to find the dwarf hunched over a workbench covered in what looks 
like intricate metalwork - three objects that resemble elaborate earpieces or 
small circlets, connected by gossamer-thin silver wires to a central crystalline 
matrix.
He looks up, sees Johannes, and his face splits into a huge grin.
"JOHANNES CONSTANTINIUS! And companions! Perfect timing - 
PERFECT timing!"
He sets down his tools and gestures excitedly at the workbench.
"The Resonance Network. Phase 1. It WORKS."
 
KELDIN'S PROGRESS REPORT
He picks up one of the devices - an elegant silver earpiece with a small crystal 
embedded in it, connected to what looks like a delicate chain that would loop 
around the ear.
"2.5 months of work. Trial, error, breakthrough, more error, more 
breakthrough. But I've cracked Phase 1."
THE PROTOTYPE - RESONANCE NETWORK MARK I:
Design:
*	Three matched devices (earpieces with embedded crystals)
*	Each crystal is linked to the others through sympathetic resonance
*	Worn on the ear (comfortable, doesn't interfere with helmets or hoods)
*	Powered by ambient magical energy - no charges, no daily limits
Capabilities:
*	Silent communication between all three wearers
*	Always-on connection - no activation needed, just think and speak
*	Range: 1 mile currently (Keldin believes he can extend to 5 miles 
with refinement)
*	Telepathic or subvocal - can either think words or whisper them, 
transmission is silent to recipients
*	No language barrier - intent is transmitted, not words (you think in 
Common, recipient "hears" in whatever language they understand)
Limitations:
*	Only works between the three specific devices
*	Cannot add new users without creating new matched sets
*	Interference in areas of heavy magical activity (like active spell battles)
*	Requires line of effect (can't penetrate lead, thick stone, or anti-magic 
fields)
 
KELDIN'S DEMONSTRATION
"Here - try them. Each of you take one."
He hands Johannes, Cyrus, and Kessa each an earpiece. They're surprisingly 
light, warm to the touch, and fit comfortably.
"Now, Johannes - think something. Direct it at Cyrus."
Johannes thinks clearly: "Can you hear this?"
Cyrus's eyes widen. "Yes! I heard you - not out loud, but in my head. Clear 
as if you'd spoken."
Kessa: "Wait, I heard it too. All three of us are connected?"
Keldin nods enthusiastically. "Exactly! Any transmission goes to ALL 
wearers simultaneously. Perfect for coordinated operations. When you're 
infiltrating a keep, spread across a battlefield, or split up for reconnaissance - 
you maintain constant communication."
He demonstrates the range by having Kessa walk outside - she can still 
communicate clearly from 200 feet away.
 
PHASE 2 & 3 UPDATE
Keldin brings out his project journal, showing detailed notes and diagrams.
"Phase 2 - Image Transmission:"
"This is proving more difficult. Transmitting thoughts and words - that's 
relatively straightforward sympathetic magic. But transmitting vision? That 
requires scrying-level enchantments integrated into the resonance matrix."
"I've made progress, but I estimate another 6-8 months for Phase 2. The 
technical challenge is immense - essentially creating a scrying sensor that 
moves with the wearer and transmits to others in real-time."
Current estimate for Phase 2: 8-10 months total from project start
"Phase 3 - Scalability:"
"This is actually easier than Phase 2. Once I have the core enchantment 
schema perfected, creating additional matched sets is mostly craftsmanship 
and materials. Each additional 3-device set would cost approximately 1,200-
1,500 gold and take 2-3 weeks to craft."
"The real breakthrough is the central resonance matrix - once that's perfected, 
it's replicable."
 
THE OFFER
Keldin looks at Johannes seriously.
"These three devices - the Mark I prototypes - are YOURS. Take 
them. Field test them. I need to know how they perform in actual 
operations - stress testing, combat conditions, magical 
interference, all of it."
"Use them for a month, then report back. Tell me what works, what 
fails, what needs improvement. That feedback will be invaluable 
for Phase 2 development and for refining the Mark I design."
"And honestly? You three NEED this. After what I've heard about 
your operations - Dargaard Keep, fighting death knights, naval 
assaults - coordinated silent communication could save your lives."
He extends the three devices toward you.
"Mark I Resonance Network. Prototype testing phase. No 
additional cost - you've already funded development. These are 
yours."
 
JOHANNES, CYRUS, KESSA - RESPONSE?
This is a major tactical upgrade:
*	Silent communication during stealth operations
*	Coordinate in combat without enemies hearing
*	Split party reconnaissance while maintaining contact
*	Emergency calls for help without alerting enemies
*	1-mile range covers most operational areas
Do you:
1.	Accept the prototypes - take them, test them, provide feedback
2.	Decline - wait for Phase 2 completion before field testing
3.	Negotiate terms - discuss specific testing parameters
4.	Ask questions - clarify functionality, limitations, concerns
What's your response?
Accept them.
Dec 10
ACCEPTING THE RESONANCE NETWORK MARK I
Johannes takes the three devices, examining his closely. The craftsmanship is 
exceptional - elegant silver work, a crystal that pulses faintly with warm light, 
surprisingly comfortable when worn.
"We'll field test them thoroughly. Palanthas research mission, then whatever 
comes after. You'll have detailed feedback within the month."
Keldin grins broadly. "Excellent! I knew you'd see the value. Now, some 
practical notes for field use:"
 
OPERATIONAL GUIDELINES
Activation:
*	Simply wear the earpiece - it attunes to you within minutes
*	No command word, no activation ritual
*	Connection establishes automatically when all three devices are worn
Usage:
*	Think clearly what you want to transmit - focus on the intended 
message
*	Can transmit to all wearers simultaneously (default)
*	Cannot selectively transmit to only one wearer (Mark I limitation - Mark 
II might address this)
*	Subvocal option: Whisper quietly, device amplifies and transmits
Range & Limitations:
*	1 mile current range (tested extensively)
*	Line of effect required - cannot penetrate: lead, 10+ feet of solid 
stone, anti-magic fields
*	Magical interference: Heavy active spellcasting nearby may cause 
static or brief interruptions
*	Emotional bleed: Strong emotions may leak through unintentionally 
(fear, panic, pain) - maintain mental discipline
Maintenance:
*	Crystals self-sustaining, draw ambient magical energy
*	Clean with soft cloth if dusty
*	Avoid submersion in water (they'll work, but connection may weaken 
temporarily)
*	If damaged, return immediately for repair
Security:
*	Connection is encrypted through sympathetic resonance - cannot be 
intercepted
*	If one device is destroyed, other two still function together
*	If device is stolen, thief cannot use it (attuned to original wearer)
*	Can be un-attuned by removing for 24 hours
 
KELDIN'S FINAL ADVICE
"Practice using them during your travel to Palanthas. Get comfortable with the 
mental discipline of targeted thought-communication versus just general 
thinking. You don't want to accidentally broadcast 'I really need to piss' to 
your entire team during a stealth infiltration."
He chuckles, then becomes more serious.
"These devices represent months of my life's work and your significant 
investment. They're prototypes, yes, but they're also the foundation of 
something revolutionary. Use them well. Keep them safe. And Johannes - your 
feedback will directly shape Phase 2 development."
"You're not just testing equipment. You're helping create the future 
of tactical communication on Krynn."
 
CYRUS TESTS HIS DEVICE
Brother Cyrus puts on his earpiece, and after a moment of concentration, his 
voice comes through clearly in Johannes and Kessa's minds:
"Mishakal's grace... this is extraordinary. Silent communication during 
healing operations, coordinating divine support during combat, calling for 
help without alerting enemies... Johannes, this changes everything."
KESSA'S ASSESSMENT
She adjusts hers, testing the fit while moving quickly through combat stances.
"Doesn't interfere with my hood or movement. Light enough I barely notice 
it. This is going to make reconnaissance SO much easier - I can scout ahead 
and report without hand signals or risking sound."
She grins. "Though we definitely need to practice not broadcasting every 
random thought. I do NOT want you two hearing my internal commentary 
about bad tavern food or annoying NPCs."
 
PAYMENT & GRATITUDE
Keldin waves off any additional payment. "You've already funded the entire 
project. These prototypes are part of that investment. Just bring me back good 
data."
"Now go - you said you're heading to Palanthas? Research mission? Be careful. 
That city's neutral, but that just means the Dragon Army and resistance are 
BOTH operating there covertly. Keep your heads down."
He walks you to the door, then pauses.
"And Johannes? Thank you. For believing in this project. For funding work 
that others would call impossible. If the Resonance Network succeeds - when 
it succeeds - it's because you saw the potential and invested in it."
"May the gods watch over you."
 
DEPARTURE FROM AK-THYLN

DAYS 4-10: TRAVEL TO PALANTHAS
During the journey, you practice using the Resonance Network:
Day 4-5: Basic communication practice - learning to think clearly and 
deliberately Day 6: Range testing - Kessa scouts 3/4 mile ahead, connection 
holds clearly Day 7: Combat coordination practice - mock scenarios with 
tactical callouts Day 8: Emotional discipline - learning to not broadcast stray 
thoughts Day 9-10: Advanced techniques - simultaneous reports, urgent 
interrupts, maintaining connection under stress
By the time you approach Palanthas, all three of you are proficient with the 
devices. The silent communication feels natural, intuitive, and incredibly 
useful.
 
DAY 11: ARRIVAL AT PALANTHAS
The great neutral city rises before you - 50,000 residents, impressive walls, 
the Great Library's towers visible even from miles away. Dragon Army 
presence is evident but subtle - patrols in the streets, officers in taverns, but 
no overt occupation.
You have:
*	Warehouse 47 (secure base)
*	Contact: Grimbold Ironfoot (caretaker)
*	Mission: Research primordial fragments + investigate Dragon Army 
interest in you
*	Resonance Network for coordination
*	Two weeks timeline
Do you want to:
1.	Go directly to Warehouse 47 - establish base, talk to Grimbold
2.	Visit Great Library first - begin research immediately
3.	Reconnaissance - scout the city, assess Dragon Army presence
4.	Something else
What's your approach?
Great library, then the warehouse. Send a runner to let Ironfoot know we're in 
town and get the quarters ready for us.
Dec 10
ARRIVAL AT PALANTHAS - GREAT LIBRARY FIRST
PRACTICAL ARRANGEMENT:
As you enter Palanthas through the main gate (2 gp entry tax paid), Kessa 
spots a street urchin - maybe 12 years old, quick-eyed, clearly looking for 
work.
She tosses him 5 silver pieces. "Know Warehouse 47 in the Eastdock Quarter?"
The boy nods eagerly. "Yes ma'am! Corner lot, three stories, dwarf caretaker!"
"Run there. Tell Grimbold Ironfoot that his employers have arrived and need 
quarters prepared for three. Go now, and there's another 5 silver when we 
arrive and confirm you delivered the message."
The boy sprints off immediately.
Via Resonance Network, Kessa thinks to the group: "Testing the devices 
in an urban environment. Can you both hear me clearly despite all 
the city noise and activity?"
Johannes and Cyrus both confirm - the connection is crystal clear despite 
being surrounded by 50,000 people, street vendors, and general city chaos.
 
THE GREAT LIBRARY OF PALANTHAS - EARLY AFTERNOON
The Library dominates the Scholar's Quarter - a massive structure of white 
marble and soaring towers, pre-Cataclysm architecture that survived intact. 
Scholars in various robes move in and out constantly.
At the entrance, two guards (city watch, not Dragon Army) check visitors:
"State your business."
Johannes presents Commander Laurana's letter of introduction:
"To whom it may concern: The bearers of this letter - Johannes 
Constantinius, Kessa Darrow, and Brother Cyrus - are authorized historical 
consultants working on matters of regional security. They are granted full 
cooperation in accessing historical archives as needed. - Commander 
Laurana, Haven Resistance."
The guard reads it, exchanges a glance with his partner, then stamps it with 
the Library's seal.
"Resistance credentials are honored here. Palanthas is neutral, but 
we're not blind to what's happening in the world. Master Aldric 
Brightquill is in the Historical Archives, third floor, west wing. Tell 
the desk clerk you have authorization."
He returns the letter. "Welcome to the Great Library. Knowledge serves all 
who seek it honestly."
 
INTERIOR - THE GREAT LIBRARY
The main hall is breathtaking:
*	Vaulted ceilings 60 feet high
*	Thousands of books on shelves reaching toward the ceiling
*	Magical lights floating throughout (permanent Light spells)
*	Dozens of scholars reading, researching, taking notes
*	The smell of old parchment, leather bindings, and ink
*	Quiet reverence - this is a temple to knowledge
At the main desk, a human clerk looks up. "How may the Library serve you?"
"We're here to see Master Aldric Brightquill. We have 
authorization and a prior relationship - we donated pre-Cataclysm 
documents several months ago."
The clerk checks a registry. "Ah yes, the Thoradin's Hall documents. Master 
Aldric speaks of those often. Third floor, Historical Archives. I'll send word 
you're coming."
 
THIRD FLOOR - HISTORICAL ARCHIVES
This section is more restricted - fewer scholars, more security, older and more 
valuable texts. A junior archivist leads you through rows of ancient 
manuscripts to a private study room.
Master Aldric Brightquill looks up from a desk covered in open books and 
scrolls. He's in his sixties, human, thin and scholarly, with ink-stained fingers 
and spectacles perched on his nose.
His face lights up with recognition.
"Johannes! Brother Cyrus! And Kessa, yes? The generous donors 
who brought us those magnificent pre-Cataclysm administrative 
records!"
He stands, gesturing enthusiastically. "Those documents have been 
INVALUABLE. We've learned so much about pre-Cataclysm governance, trade 
routes, military organization. Several papers have been published based on 
your contribution!"
He clears space at a large research table. "Please, sit! What brings you back to 
Palanthas? More donations? Or are you seeking knowledge this time?"
 
JOHANNES - HOW DO YOU FRAME YOUR REQUEST?
You need information on:
1.	Primordial fragments (ancient entities predating the gods)
2.	Binding/sealing rituals (how ancient priests imprisoned such 
entities)
3.	Specifically related to Xak Tsaroth (Temple of Huerzyd, pre-
Kingpriest era)
Do you:
A) Full Disclosure
*	Explain exactly what happened at Xak Tsaroth
*	Admit you accidentally released a primordial fragment
*	Request urgent research assistance
B) Academic Interest
*	Frame it as "historical research into pre-Cataclysm containment magic"
*	Don't mention the recent release
*	Keep it theoretical
C) Partial Truth
*	Mention that a dangerous entity has been discovered
*	Imply it's still contained but needs better understanding
*	Request research without admitting your role
D) Something else

Dec 10
FULL DISCLOSURE TO MASTER ALDRIC
Johannes leans forward, his expression serious.
"Master Aldric, we're not here for academic curiosity. We're here because we 
have an urgent, active threat that requires your expertise."
He lays out the situation methodically:
*	Dragon Army excavating beneath Xak Tsaroth's Temple of Huerzyd
*	Discovery of ancient seals imprisoning something pre-divine
*	Sabotage operation to stop the Dragon Army
*	Accidental breach of the final seals during flooding
*	Release of what appears to be a primordial fragment
*	Entity currently dormant at excavation site but potentially dangerous
*	Need for information on binding/re-sealing rituals
"We released it accidentally while stopping a worse outcome - the 
Dragon Army controlling it. But it's free now, and we need to 
understand what it is and how to re-contain it before it becomes 
active."
 
MASTER ALDRIC'S REACTION
The elderly scholar goes very still as Johannes speaks. His expression shifts 
from enthusiasm to concern to something approaching horror.
When Johannes finishes, Aldric removes his spectacles, cleans them slowly (a 
nervous habit), then puts them back on.
"A primordial fragment. From beneath the Temple of Huerzyd. 
Released after three centuries of containment."
He stands abruptly and begins pacing, muttering to himself:
"Huerzyd... Huerzyd... pre-Kingpriest... that's Age of Dreams era, 
possibly earlier... Temple dedicated to a struck god... containment 
specialists..."
He stops, turns to face you.
"You're telling me that beneath Xak Tsaroth - a city destroyed by 
divine judgment during the Cataclysm - there was an OLDER 
threat? Something the ancient priests couldn't destroy and could 
only imprison? And it's now free?"
Cyrus nods. "Yes. And it's currently dormant at the excavation site. But we 
don't know for how long, or what might trigger it to become active."
Aldric sits heavily. "This is... this is extraordinary. Terrifying, but 
extraordinary. The academic implications alone... but more importantly, the 
immediate danger."
He looks at Johannes with newfound respect.
"You came here immediately to research solutions rather than 
simply reporting and washing your hands of it. That's... that's 
responsible. Admirable, even."
"Very well. You need information on primordial fragments and 
binding rituals. I'll help you. But understand - this kind of research 
requires access to the RESTRICTED archives. The dangerous 
knowledge section. Materials we don't let just anyone examine."
 
RESTRICTED ARCHIVES ACCESS
Aldric stands and begins gathering materials.
"I'm the Chief Historian. I have authority to grant restricted access 
for legitimate research purposes. And if preventing a primordial 
entity from potentially destroying half of Ansalon isn't legitimate, I 
don't know what is."
He writes out an authorization on official Library parchment:
"Authorization for Restricted Archives Access - Level 3 (Ancient Threats & 
Containment Protocols). Granted to Johannes Constantinius, Kessa Darrow, 
Brother Cyrus. Duration: Two weeks. Purpose: Research primordial entities 
and binding rituals. Authorized by Master Aldric Brightquill, Chief 
Historian."
He stamps it with his personal seal.
"This grants you access to materials that would normally require 
months of academic credentials to see. Use it wisely. And please - 
DON'T steal anything or damage the texts. Some of these are 
literally irreplaceable."
 
WHAT ALDRIC KNOWS (Initial Overview)
"I'm not an expert in primordial entities - that's extremely esoteric 
knowledge. But I know where to START looking. Let me give you 
the overview before we dive into the archives:"
PRIMORDIAL FRAGMENTS:
"Before the gods of Krynn shaped the world, there was... chaos. Raw creation. 
Unbound potential. The gods gave that chaos FORM, PURPOSE, ORDER. But 
they couldn't unmake what existed before them - they could only shape it, 
bind it, contain it."
"Primordial fragments are pieces of that original chaos. They don't think as we 
understand thinking. They don't have desires or goals. They simply ARE. They 
exist. They react. They consume."
"The ancient priests - this would be Age of Dreams, maybe 2,000-3,000 years 
ago - discovered some of these fragments and realized they couldn't destroy 
them. So they IMPRISONED them in specially constructed containment sites, 
usually beneath temples, guarded by divine authority."
THE TEMPLE OF HUERZYD:
"Huerzyd... I know that name. Give me a moment."
He pulls a reference tome from his personal shelf, flips through it.
"Here. Temple of Huerzyd. Dedicated to a god whose name was 
STRUCK from history during the Second Dragon War. The god fell 
- not died, but FELL. Became corrupt, twisted, cast down by the 
other deities."
"The temple priests who served that god were left without divine patron. But 
they were experts in one thing: BINDING. Containing. Imprisoning things 
that shouldn't exist. They became... specialists in dangerous knowledge."
"When the Kingpriest rose to power centuries later, he ordered their works 
destroyed, their knowledge burned, their temples sealed. Xak Tsaroth's 
Temple of Huerzyd was sealed approximately 1,000 years before the 
Cataclysm."
"If there's a primordial fragment imprisoned there, it's been contained for at 
LEAST 1,000 years, possibly 2,000 or more."
 
THE RESEARCH PLAN
Aldric lays out a strategy:
"We need to find three things:
1. IDENTIFICATION - What specific type of primordial fragment is this?
*	Look for: Historical records of entities imprisoned beneath Xak Tsaroth
*	Sources: Pre-Kingpriest temple archives, Dragon War era texts
*	Expected time: 1-2 days
2. BINDING RITUALS - How did the priests originally contain it?
*	Look for: Containment protocols from the Temple of Huerzyd
*	Sources: Forbidden ritual texts, containment theory treatises
*	Expected time: 2-3 days
3. RE-SEALING METHODS - How do we put it back?
*	Look for: Modern applications of ancient binding magic
*	Sources: Divine magic theory, clerical dissertations, possibly 
consultation with high priests
*	Expected time: 3-5 days
Total research estimate: 1 week of intensive study, possibly 10 days 
if we hit complications."
 
ALDRIC'S OFFER
"I'll personally assist with this research. This is too important and 
too dangerous to leave to junior scholars. I'll guide you through the 
restricted archives, help interpret ancient texts, and provide 
context for what we find."
"Additionally, I'll send discrete inquiries to other archives - Tarsis has some 
pre-Cataclysm materials, and there's a private collector in Palanthas who 
specializes in dangerous knowledge. Between the Library, those sources, and 
your own investigative skills, we should be able to assemble what you need."
He looks at you seriously.
"This is academic work. Long hours, difficult texts, tedious 
research. Not glamorous. But if we succeed, we might save 
thousands of lives. Are you prepared for that?"
 
PRACTICAL ARRANGEMENTS
Aldric continues:
"The Library closes to general public at sunset, but researchers with 
authorization can work through the night in the restricted archives. I 
recommend you establish your lodging, get settled, then return tomorrow 
morning. We'll begin systematic research then."
"Where are you staying in Palanthas?"
When you mention Warehouse 47:
"Ah, Eastdock Quarter. Excellent location - close enough to reach the Library 
quickly but far enough from Old City politics. Smart."
He provides you with research tokens - small bronze medallions that grant 
unrestricted access to the Library during your authorized period.
"Return tomorrow at dawn. We'll begin with the identification 
research. Bring patience and strong tea - this will be intensive 
work."

EASTDOCK QUARTER - LATE AFTERNOON
The party makes their way through Palanthas toward the docks. The city is

oppressive - officers in taverns, patrols on corners, but maintaining the fiction 
of Palanthas's neutrality.
Via Resonance Network, Kessa thinks: "Three Dragon Army soldiers

traffic. Casual observation or looking for someone?"
Johannes responds: "Keep moving naturally. Don't give them reason 
to focus on us."
You pass without incident - the soldiers barely glance at you. Just three more 
travelers among thousands.
 
WAREHOUSE 47 - ARRIVAL
The familiar three-story building comes into view on its corner lot. Looks 
exactly as you left it months ago - well-maintained, sturdy, the loading dock 
intact.
The street urchin you sent ahead is waiting outside, practically bouncing with 
excitement. "I delivered your message! The dwarf said everything's ready! He 
gave me an extra silver for running fast!"
Kessa hands him the promised 5 silver. "Well done. Now get lost before 
someone decides you're loitering."
The boy grins and sprints off, rich by street urchin standards.
 
INTERIOR - GRIMBOLD'S GREETING
The door opens before you knock. Grimbold Ironfoot stands there - stocky 
dwarf, practical work clothes, discrete and competent as always.
"Welcome back, employers. Your message gave me thirty minutes' warning. 
Upper floors are prepared - three rooms cleaned, beds made, water heated, 
supplies stocked. I assume you're here on business, not tourism?"
His eyes flick to the street briefly - checking if you were followed - then ushers 
you inside and locks the door.
Ground Floor:
*	Everything as you left it
*	Clean, organized, well-maintained
*	Loading dock secure
*	Side entrance functional
*	Grimbold's been an excellent caretaker
"Let's talk upstairs. Ground floor has too many sightlines from the 
street."
 
SECOND FLOOR - SECURE BRIEFING
Grimbold leads you to the large central room on the second floor, closes the 
door, and speaks quietly:
"First things first: Dragon Army has been asking about this 
warehouse. Started about three weeks ago."
He pulls out a small journal with notes.
"Three separate inquiries:
1. Dragon Army administrative officer - came to the Harbormaster's 
office, requested property records for 'recently acquired warehouses in 
Eastdock Quarter.' Your deed transaction showed up in those records. They 
know THREE individuals purchased this property jointly several months ago.
2. Dragon Army intelligence agent (civilian clothes, but I recognized the 
type) - came here directly, claimed to be a prospective buyer, asked about the 
owners. I told him the owners are 'traveling merchants' and provided no 
names.
3. Street informants - local kids have been asking dockworkers about 'three 
foreigners who own Warehouse 47.' Someone's paying for information."
He looks at you seriously. "They're looking for you specifically. They 
don't have your names yet - or if they do, they haven't connected 
them to this property - but they know THREE people matching 
general descriptions purchased this warehouse after significant 
activity in this region."
"Timeline matches: Pax Tharkas liberation, Flotsam fleet 
destruction, Palanthas dock rescue. You've been active, successful, 
and someone in Dragon Army intelligence has noticed the pattern."
 
GRIMBOLD'S ASSESSMENT
"Current threat level: MODERATE."
"They're investigating, but not actively hunting. No raids, no surveillance 
teams, no aggressive action. Just... gathering information. Which means 
they're building a case or a profile before they act."
"My recommendation: Keep low profile while you're here. Don't advertise your 
presence. The warehouse is secure - I've added some basic wards and alarm 
bells. But if Dragon Army intelligence decides this property is worth a closer 
look, those won't stop a determined investigation."
He crosses his arms. "What brought you back to Palanthas? And is it 
going to increase Dragon Army attention or decrease it?"

FULL DISCLOSURE TO GRIMBOLD
Johannes lays out the situation methodically - Xak Tsaroth excavation,

Grimbold listens without interruption, his expression growing more serious.

He strokes his beard thoughtfully. "Well, at least you're not boring 
employers."
 
GRIMBOLD'S TACTICAL ASSESSMENT
"First question: Is there a discrete exit outside of visuals? Like 
through the basement?"
Grimbold nods. "Yes, actually. Let me show you."
He leads you down to the ground floor, then to a corner near the loading dock. 
He moves several crates aside, revealing a trapdoor.
"Basement - original construction, pre-Cataclysm. When I took 
over as caretaker, I explored thoroughly."
 
THE BASEMENT
Down a wooden ladder into a stone-walled chamber - dry, cool, approximately 
30 feet by 40 feet. Storage space, mostly empty now.
But Grimbold leads you to the far wall and presses a specific stone. A section 
of wall swings inward - hidden door, well-maintained hinges.
"Smuggler's tunnel. Pre-Cataclysm merchants used these all over 
Eastdock. This one runs 80 feet east, exits into an abandoned 
building three lots over. I've kept it maintained but haven't 
advertised its existence."
He lights a lantern and leads you through - low tunnel, shored up with timber, 
dry and stable. Emerges in the cellar of a dilapidated warehouse that appears 
abandoned from street level.
"Exit here, you're three buildings away from Warehouse 47. No 
direct sightline. Anyone watching your warehouse won't see you 
leave. I use this for... discrete errands."
Back in your basement: "So yes, you have a hidden exit. I recommend 
using it for your Library trips. Enter and leave Warehouse 47 
publicly once or twice to maintain appearances, but do your actual 
research comings and goings through the tunnel."
 
GRIMBOLD'S RESPONSE TO THE DECOY IDEA
"Second question: Actors to replicate you lazing about on the 
second and third floors?"
Grimbold grins - first genuine smile you've seen from him.
"Now THAT is thinking like a professional. Yes, I can arrange that. 
Eastdock has plenty of out-of-work sailors and dockworkers who'd 
appreciate easy coin for sitting around visible in windows."
His proposal:
"Give me until tomorrow afternoon. I'll hire three people - rough 
matches for your builds and general appearance. They don't need 
to be perfect; they just need to be visible from the street at regular 
intervals."
Casting requirements:
*	Johannes stand-in: Human male, tall, dark-haired, similar build
*	Kessa stand-in: Human female, lean build, hooded when visible
*	Cyrus stand-in: Human male, clerical robes, holy symbol visible
"I'll brief them: 'Three traveling merchants renting the warehouse, 
keeping irregular hours, want privacy.' They'll appear in windows 
periodically, move around the building, maintain the illusion of 
occupation. They won't enter the basement or touch anything 
sensitive - just visible presence."
Cost: 5 gold per day for all three (covers their wages plus 
Grimbold's arrangement fee)
Timeline: Can have them in place by tomorrow afternoon, 
maintain for as long as you need
"Meanwhile, YOU three use the tunnel for actual movements. 
Anyone watching sees 'three occupants' maintaining normal 
patterns, while you're actually conducting research and operations 
the Dragon Army doesn't know about."
 
GRIMBOLD'S ADDITIONAL ADVICE
"Regarding Dragon Army surveillance, here's what I know from

Current Dragon Army Focus:
*	They're trying to connect incidents: Pax Tharkas, Flotsam, possibly 
others
*	Looking for a "specialized resistance cell" - small, elite, highly effective
*	Don't have names yet, but they have descriptions: "two humans and a 
cleric," "three-person team with unusual capabilities"
*	Their intelligence network in Palanthas is good but not omniscient
Grimbold's Recommendations:
1. Vary your appearance when moving through the city
*	Kessa: Different cloak colors, vary the hood
*	Johannes: Add/remove hat, change coat
*	Cyrus: Hide holy symbol when not needed, wear civilian clothes 
occasionally
*	"Not disguises, just... not looking EXACTLY like the descriptions every

2. Split up for some movements
*	"Three people together is memorable. One or two is normal city traffic."

3. Avoid patterns
*	"Don't leave at the same time every day, don't take the same route"

4. Establish cover story
*	"If questioned directly: you're historical consultants researching trade

*	"Boring, academic, explains Library visits, gives you reason to be here"

*	"Rally point: The Broken Keel tavern, two blocks south - discrete,

GRIMBOLD'S FINAL QUESTION
"Two weeks of research, decoy actors, discrete movements, and

connect Johannes Constantinius and companions to Warehouse 47

"I'm not afraid of Dragon Army attention, but I need to know the

JOHANNES - YOUR RESPONSE:

7:06 AM
RESEARCH PHASE - FAST RESOLUTION
Over the next seven days, Johannes, Cyrus, and Kessa work intensively in the 
Great Library's restricted archives with Master Aldric's guidance. Long hours 
of ancient texts, pre-Cataclysm records, and dangerous knowledge yield 
results.
 
WHAT YOU LEARNED:
THE ENTITY - IDENTIFIED:
The primordial fragment beneath Xak Tsaroth is called an "Unbound" - a 
piece of raw elemental chaos from before divine shaping. Specifically, this one 
is a water-aspected chaos fragment (explains the blue-green light, the 
affinity for the flooded excavation).
*	Nature: Pre-divine, non-sentient, reactive rather than proactive
*	Behavior: Feeds on psychic energy (memories, emotions, 
consciousness)
*	Dormancy: After feeding, enters dormant state until disturbed
*	Threat Level: If fully active, could devastate a 50-mile radius by 
unmaking reality's structure
*	Current Status: Dormant after feeding on Dragon Army casualties, 
stable unless provoked
THE ORIGINAL BINDING:
The Temple of Huerzyd priests used a Threefold Seal:
1.	Physical Seal: Stone barriers inscribed with containment runes (now 
broken by excavation)
2.	Divine Seal: Wards powered by divine authority (weakened when the 
god fell, degraded over 1,000+ years)
3.	Sacrifice Seal: Voluntary binding by a priest who remained as eternal 
guardian (died during Cataclysm, seal broke)
All three seals failed when the Dragon Army breached the chamber and the 
Cataclysm's flooding damaged the already-weakened wards.
THE SOLUTION - RE-SEALING:
You cannot recreate the original Threefold Seal (no fallen god to provide 
divine authority, no priest willing to sacrifice themselves eternally).
BUT: You found an alternative in a treatise on "Emergency Containment 
Protocols for Divine Catastrophes":
The Eternal Tomb Method
Requirements:
1.	Divine Authority: High Priest or Disk Bearer invoking direct divine 
power
2.	Ritual Components: Sanctified stone (from a consecrated temple), 
holy water (blessed by multiple gods), silver chains (representing 
binding)
3.	Physical Collapse: Bury the entity under massive weight of blessed 
stone and earth
4.	Sustained Consecration: Maintain permanent Hallow spell on the 
site
Process:
*	Divine authority casts Hallow on the excavation site (24-hour ritual, 
1,000 gp components)
*	While ritual is active, collapse the excavation using mundane means 
(explosives, structural sabotage)
*	The Hallow effect becomes permanent, binding the entity beneath 
consecrated ground
*	Entity remains dormant, contained by divine authority and physical 
weight
*	Requires annual renewal by a cleric (simple maintenance ritual)
Success Rate: 95% effective for dormant entities, 60% for active ones
Timeline: Must be executed while entity is dormant (current state, but 
unknown duration)
 
MASTER ALDRIC'S ASSESSMENT:
"This is achievable. You need a high-ranking cleric - Goldmoon with the Disks 
would be ideal, or Elistan as High Priest of Paladine. The ritual itself is 
straightforward if expensive. The structural collapse is engineering, not 
magic."
"Recommendation: Return to Haven, brief Commander Laurana, coordinate 
with Goldmoon for the Hallow casting, organize engineering corps to collapse 
the excavation. Execute within two weeks before the entity becomes active 
again."
 
ADDITIONAL DISCOVERY - IMPORTANT WARNING:
In a personal journal from a Temple of Huerzyd priest, you found this entry:
"The Unbound does not forget. Those who freed it from imprisonment - 
intentionally or otherwise - are MARKED. It will recognize their psychic 
signature if encountered again. Approach with caution."
Translation: The entity "remembers" Johannes, Cyrus, and Kessa at some 
fundamental level. If you're present during re-sealing, it may react to your 
presence. Recommend staying at distance while Goldmoon performs the 
ritual.

MASTER KELDIN'S WORKSHOP - AFTERNOON
The dwarf looks up from his workbench as you enter, grinning broadly.
"Back already? How did the Mark I prototypes perform?"
 
RESONANCE NETWORK FIELD TEST REPORT
Johannes provides comprehensive feedback:
SUCCESSES:
*	Silent communication during urban operations (Palanthas)
*	Crystal clear transmission despite city noise and activity
*	1-mile range confirmed multiple times
*	No accidental eavesdropping or interception detected
*	Comfortable to wear for extended periods (7+ days continuous use)
*	No interference from general magical activity
*	Emotional discipline learned quickly - minimal accidental thought 
broadcasting after initial practice
STRENGTHS:
*	Always-on connection invaluable for coordination
*	Subvocal option works perfectly for discrete communication
*	No daily limits or charges needed
*	Lightweight, doesn't interfere with combat or stealth
LIMITATIONS CONFIRMED:
*	Cannot selectively transmit to one wearer (all three receive 
simultaneously)
*	Brief static when passing through areas of heavy ambient magic
*	Requires conscious thought-discipline to avoid broadcasting stray ideas
*	Line of effect requirement means thick stone walls (10+ feet) do block 
signal
RECOMMENDATIONS FOR MARK II:
*	Selective transmission option (choose recipient rather than broadcast to 
all)
*	Slightly extended range (1.5-2 miles would be ideal)
*	Visual indicator when connection is active/inactive
*	Emergency "silent mode" that blocks all transmission temporarily
 
KELDIN'S RESPONSE
He takes notes furiously, nodding and grinning.
"Excellent feedback! Exactly what I needed. The selective transmission - that's 
technically challenging but definitely achievable for Mark II. Visual indicator 
is simple - I can add a tiny crystal that glows when active."
He examines the devices as you return them briefly for inspection.
"No physical damage, crystals still perfectly attuned, enchantments stable. 
These performed flawlessly. You've validated the core design."
He hands them back. "Keep them. They're yours. Mark I is proven technology 
now. When I develop Mark II with improvements, I'll offer you an upgrade, 
but these will serve you well until then."
PROJECT STATUS UPDATE:
"Phase 2 - Image Transmission: Still working on it. The scrying integration is 
proving more complex than anticipated. Current estimate: 8-10 months from 
project start (so 5-7 more months)."
"But based on Mark I's success, I'm confident Phase 2 is achievable. Your field 
test proved the fundamental resonance network is sound. Adding visual 
transmission is just... very complicated engineering."
He walks you to the door. "Thank you. For funding this, for field testing, for 
providing real operational feedback. The Resonance Network will change 
tactical communication across Krynn, and it's happening because you believed 
in it."

7:49 AM
YES - CLAUDE PRO MESSAGE LIMITS
Claude Pro has a message limit that resets weekly (exact number varies 
but it's significant - usually enough for extensive conversations, but long 
campaigns can hit it).
When you're approaching the limit, you'll see warnings. Once hit, you need to 
wait for the weekly reset.
WORKAROUNDS FOR LONG CAMPAIGNS:
1.	Start new chats periodically - What we're doing now. Compile 
summaries and continue in fresh thread.
2.	Use Projects (which you're doing) - Project knowledge persists across 
chats, so context isn't lost.
3.	Be strategic about message usage - Combine multiple 
questions/decisions in one message when possible.
4.	Save critical information - Keep your own notes/summaries as 
backup.
 
FOR THIS CAMPAIGN:
Since we're hitting limits and about to start a three-mission arc, this is the 
PERFECT time to:
1.	Compile comprehensive summary (next message)
2.	Start fresh thread for Icewall Expedition
3.	Reference this thread's summary in new chat
Should I create the final summary document now so you can start 
the new thread with it?
It'll include everything you need: character sheets, inventory, relationships, 
plot threads, mission briefing for Icewall.
